<span class=\"acc-arrow arrow-up\"></span></h3>\n                    <div class=\"pdp_faq acc-active\" a_index=\"0\" style=\"padding: 0px; margin: 0px; overflow: hidden;\"><p></p><div style=\"text-align: justify;\">Extensive planning and designing is required to implement an effective network. This course helps participant to understand the planning concepts and to use them to design a network appropriately.<br>\n<br>\nSimplilearn’s ‘Designing and Implementing a Server Infrastructure’ course covers key concepts of the new Windows Server 2012 and 2012 R2 platforms. It also provides a guide to use existing and new features to design a network architecture. This course helps participants gain knowledge on the technologies required to implement them in the organization.</div><p></p></div>\n                </li>\n                                <li>\n                    <h3>Why is the certification most sought-after? <span class=\"acc-arrow arrow-down\"></span></h3>\n                    <div class=\"pdp_faq\" a_index=\"1\" style=\"padding: 0px; margin: 0px; overflow: hidden; height: 0px;\"><p></p><div style=\"text-align: justify;\">The certification is sought-after for the following reasons:</div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">It is a globally recognized professional certification</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Microsoft certification is valid across industries</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Provides proficiency in implementing server infrastructure</li>\n</ul><p></p></div>\n                </li>\n                                <li>\n                    <h3>What learning benefits do you get from Simplilearn’s training? <span class=\"acc-arrow arrow-down\"></span></h3>\n                    <div class=\"pdp_faq\" a_index=\"2\" style=\"padding: 0px; margin: 0px; overflow: hidden; height: 0px;\"><p></p><div style=\"text-align: justify;\">By the end of Simplilearn’s training, participants will be able to understand the following techniques:</div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Plan and deploy a server infrastructure</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Design and implement Network Infrastructure Services</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Design and Implement Network Access Services</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Design and Implement an Active directory infrastructure</li>\n</ul><p></p></div>\n                </li>\n                                <li>\n                    <h3>What are the career benefits in-store for you? <span class=\"acc-arrow arrow-down\"></span></h3>\n                    <div class=\"pdp_faq\" a_index=\"3\" style=\"padding: 0px; margin: 0px; overflow: hidden; height: 0px;\"><p></p><div style=\"text-align: justify;\">This course provides the participants with the following career benefits:</div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">According to bestitcertifications.org, a Software developer with a certification of Microsoft Certified Solutions Developer (MSCD) can earn $53,569 – $104,163 annually.</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">This certification is recognized in IT industry.</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">This course and certification will increase your visibility in your organization.</li>\n\t<li style=\"text-align: justify;\">This certification sets you apart from your colleagues and ensures you get recognized for your knowledge and skill.</li>\n</ul><p></p></div>\n                </li>\n                                <li>\n                    <h3>Who should do this course? <span class=\"acc-arrow arrow-down\"></span></h3>\n                    <div class=\"pdp_faq\" a_index=\"4\" style=\"padding: 0px; margin: 0px; overflow: hidden; height: 0px;\"><p></p><div style=\"text-align: justify;\">This course is designed for candidates seeking to move into designing and architecting a network rather than only implementing others’ designs. IT Admins with experience in setting up services such as AD DS, DNS, and DHCP will get introduced to new concepts as well as an update to concepts they know but in context of designing the network.</div><p></p></div>\n                </li>\n                                <li>\n                    <h3>Why Simplilearn? <span class=\"acc-arrow arrow-down\"></span></h3>\n
